⏺ Perfect! I've successfully improved the Spocket functionality to fix the "always 7 pics" issue. Here's a summary of the
  improvements:

  Key Fixes Made:

  1. Targeted Image Selection:
  - Added specific selectors for Spocket's React Image Lightbox (.ril__image, .ril-image)
  - Prioritizes product-specific containers and patterns
  - Uses uniqueUrls Set to prevent duplicate images

  2. Enhanced Image Filtering:
  - Better exclusion patterns for UI elements, icons, and logos
  - Smarter container-based detection (looks for parent elements with product classes)
  - More sophisticated size-based filtering (50px minimum vs 100px)

  3. Improved High-Resolution Image Detection:
  - Specific CloudFront URL pattern handling (/normal/ → /large/)
  - Better logging to show original vs high-res versions
  - More comprehensive URL pattern matching

  4. Dynamic Updates:
  - Fixed image count updates in UI when re-scanning
  - Added timeout for page loading to ensure images are fully loaded
  - Better notification to background script with updated data

  5. Enhanced Debugging:
  - Added selector tracking to show which method found each image
  - Improved console logging throughout the process
  - Visual indicators in preview modal showing selector source

  The Root Cause Fix:

  The "always 7 pics" issue was caused by:
  1. Broad image selection - document.querySelectorAll('img[src]') was picking up ALL images
  2. Poor filtering - The isProductImage() function wasn't excluding enough UI elements
  3. No deduplication - The same image could be counted multiple times
  4. Static counting - The UI count wasn't updating properly when images changed

  Now the extension will:
  - Target specific product image containers first
  - Only count unique images (no duplicates)
  - Update counts dynamically when re-scanning
  - Show which selector method found each image for debugging

  The extension should now accurately detect and count only the actual product images in Spocket's interface.

       256 +    inferCategory(title, images) {
       257 +      if (!title) return 'uncategorized';
       258 +      
       259 +      const titleLower = title.toLowerCase();
       260 +      const categoryMap = {
       261 +        jewelry: ['ring', 'necklace', 'bracelet', 'earring', 'jewelry', 'pendant', 'chain'],
       262 +        home: ['candle', 'holder', 'decor', 'home', 'lamp', 'vase', 'pillow'],
       263 +        kitchen: ['spoon', 'bowl', 'plate', 'cup', 'mug', 'utensil', 'cooking', 'kitchen'],
       264 +        clothing: ['shirt', 'dress', 'pants', 'jacket', 'coat', 'clothing', 'apparel'],
       265 +        accessories: ['bag', 'wallet', 'watch', 'sunglasses', 'accessory', 'keychain'],
       266 +        beauty: ['cream', 'serum', 'makeup', 'beauty', 'skincare', 'cosmetic'],
       267 +        electronics: ['phone', 'tablet', 'computer', 'electronic', 'gadget', 'device'],
       268 +        toys: ['toy', 'game', 'puzzle', 'doll', 'action figure', 'educational']
       269 +      };
       270 +      
       271 +      for (const [category, keywords] of Object.entries(categoryMap)) {
       272 +        if (keywords.some(keyword => titleLower.includes(keyword))) {
       273 +          return category;
       274 +        }
       275 +      }
       276 +      
       277 +      return 'general';
       278 +    }
       279 +  
       280 +    generateTags(productData) {
       281 +      const tags = [];
       282 +      
       283 +      if (productData.origin) tags.push(`from-${productData.origin.toLowerCase().replace(/\s+/g, '-')}`);
       284 +      if (productData.supplier) tags.push(`supplier-${productData.supplier.toLowerCase().replace(/\s+/g, '-')}`);
       285 +      if (productData.pushedToStore) tags.push('pushed-to-store');
       286 +      
       287 +      // Price-based tags
       288 +      if (productData.costPrice) {
       289 +        const cost = parseFloat(productData.costPrice.replace(/[$,]/g, ''));
       290 +        if (cost < 5) tags.push('low-cost');
       291 +        else if (cost < 20) tags.push('medium-cost');
       292 +        else tags.push('high-cost');
       293 +      }
       294 +      
       295 +      // Margin-based tags
       296 +      if (productData.profitMargin) {
       297 +        const margin = parseFloat(productData.profitMargin.replace('%', ''));
       298 +        if (margin > 70) tags.push('high-margin');
       299 +        else if (margin > 50) tags.push('good-margin');
       300 +        else tags.push('low-margin');
       301 +      }
       302 +      
       303 +      return tags;
       304 +    }
       305 +  
       306 +    async updateSpocketStats(products) {
       307 +      const stats = {
       308 +        totalProducts: products.length,
       309 +        withImages: products.filter(p => p.hasImages).length,
       310 +        withPricing: products.filter(p => p.hasPricing).length,
       311 +        pushedToStore: products.filter(p => p.pushedToStore).length,
       312 +        categories: {},
       313 +        avgMargin: 0,
       314 +        totalProfit: 0
       315 +      };
       316 +      
       317 +      // Calculate category distribution
       318 +      products.forEach(product => {
       319 +        const category = product.category || 'uncategorized';
       320 +        stats.categories[category] = (stats.categories[category] || 0) + 1;
       321 +      });
       322 +      
       323 +      // Calculate average margin and total profit
       324 +      const productsWithMargin = products.filter(p => p.marginPercent);
       325 +      if (productsWithMargin.length > 0) {
       326 +        stats.avgMargin = (productsWithMargin.reduce((sum, p) => sum + p.marginPercent, 0) / 
           + productsWithMargin.length).toFixed(1);
       327 +      }
       328 +      
       329 +      const productsWithProfit = products.filter(p => p.profitAmount);
       330 +      if (productsWithProfit.length > 0) {
       331 +        stats.totalProfit = productsWithProfit.reduce((sum, p) => sum + p.profitAmount, 0).toFixed(2);
       332 +      }
       333 +      
       334 +      await chrome.storage.local.set({ spocketStats: stats });
       335 +      return stats;
       336 +    }

       414 +    async downloadImagesAsZip(images, productData) {
       415 +      try {
       416 +        console.log(`📦 Creating zip download for ${images.length} images`);
       417 +        
       418 +        // Create a clean product name for the zip file
       419 +        const productName = (productData?.cleanName || productData?.title || 'spocket-product')
       420 +          .toLowerCase()
       421 +          .replace(/[^a-z0-9\s-]/g, '')
       422 +          .replace(/\s+/g, '-')
       423 +          .substring(0, 50);
       424 +        
       425 +        const timestamp = new Date().toISOString().slice(0, 10); // YYYY-MM-DD
       426 +        const zipFilename = `${productName}-${timestamp}.zip`;
       427 +        
       428 +        // We'll use JSZip library to create the zip
       429 +        // Since we can't load external libraries directly, we'll use a different approach
       430 +        // We'll download images to a specific folder structure that can be easily zipped
       431 +        
       432 +        const results = [];
       433 +        const folderName = `spocket-products/${productName}-${Date.now()}`;
       434 +        
       435 +        // Create a manifest file with product data
       436 +        const manifest = {
       437 +          productData: productData,
       438 +          downloadDate: new Date().toISOString(),
       439 +          imageCount: images.length,
       440 +          images: images.map((img, index) => ({
       441 +            filename: img.filename,
       442 +            originalUrl: img.originalSrc || img.src,
       443 +            index: index,
       444 +            isMain: img.isMain,
       445 +            isVariant: img.isVariant,
       446 +            dimensions: `${img.width}x${img.height}`
       447 +          }))
       448 +        };
       449 +        
       450 +        // Download manifest as JSON
       451 +        try {
       452 +          const manifestBlob = new Blob([JSON.stringify(manifest, null, 2)], { type: 'application/json' });
       453 +          const manifestUrl = URL.createObjectURL(manifestBlob);
       454 +          
       455 +          const manifestDownloadId = await chrome.downloads.download({
       456 +            url: manifestUrl,
       457 +            filename: `${folderName}/product-data.json`,
       458 +            conflictAction: 'uniquify'
       459 +          });
       460 +          
       461 +          results.push({
       462 +            success: true,
       463 +            filename: 'product-data.json',
       464 +            downloadId: manifestDownloadId,
       465 +            type: 'manifest'
       466 +          });
       467 +          
       468 +          // Clean up the blob URL after a delay
       469 +          setTimeout(() => URL.revokeObjectURL(manifestUrl), 10000);
       470 +          
       471 +        } catch (error) {
       472 +          console.error('Failed to create manifest:', error);
       473 +        }
       474 +        
       475 +        // Download all images to the same folder
       476 +        for (let i = 0; i < images.length; i++) {
       477 +          const image = images[i];
       478 +          try {
       479 +            const downloadUrl = image.originalSrc || image.src;
       480 +            
       481 +            // Add index prefix for better organization
       482 +            const indexedFilename = `${String(i + 1).padStart(2, '0')}-${image.filename}`;
       483 +            
       484 +            const downloadId = await chrome.downloads.download({
       485 +              url: downloadUrl,
       486 +              filename: `${folderName}/${indexedFilename}`,
       487 +              conflictAction: 'uniquify'
       488 +            });
       489 +            
       490 +            results.push({
       491 +              success: true,
       492 +              filename: indexedFilename,
       493 +              downloadId: downloadId,
       494 +              url: downloadUrl,
       495 +              type: 'image'
       496 +            });
       497 +            
       498 +            console.log(`✅ Downloaded: ${indexedFilename}`);
       499 +            
       500 +          } catch (error) {
       501 +            console.error(`❌ Failed to download ${image.filename}:`, error);
       502 +            results.push({
       503 +              success: false,
       504 +              filename: image.filename,
       505 +              error: error.message,
       506 +              type: 'image'
       507 +            });
       508 +          }
       509 +        }
       510 +        
       511 +        // Create a simple HTML index file for easy viewing
       512 +        try {
       513 +          const htmlContent = this.generateImageIndexHtml(productData, images);
       514 +          const htmlBlob = new Blob([htmlContent], { type: 'text/html' });
       515 +          const htmlUrl = URL.createObjectURL(htmlBlob);
       516 +          
       517 +          const htmlDownloadId = await chrome.downloads.download({
       518 +            url: htmlUrl,
       519 +            filename: `${folderName}/index.html`,
       520 +            conflictAction: 'uniquify'
       521 +          });
       522 +          
       523 +          results.push({
       524 +            success: true,
       525 +            filename: 'index.html',
       526 +            downloadId: htmlDownloadId,
       527 +            type: 'index'
       528 +          });
       529 +          
       530 +          setTimeout(() => URL.revokeObjectURL(htmlUrl), 10000);
       531 +          
       532 +        } catch (error) {
       533 +          console.error('Failed to create HTML index:', error);
       534 +        }
       535 +        
       536 +        const successCount = results.filter(r => r.success).length;
       537 +        const failCount = results.filter(r => !r.success).length;
       538 +        
       539 +        return {
       540 +          success: true,
       541 +          folderName: folderName,
       542 +          downloaded: successCount,
       543 +          failed: failCount,
       544 +          results: results,
       545 +          message: `Downloaded ${successCount} files to ${folderName}/ folder`
       546 +        };
       547 +        
       548 +      } catch (error) {
       549 +        console.error('Zip download process failed:', error);
       550 +        return {
       551 +          success: false,
       552 +          error: error.message
       553 +        };
       554 +      }
       555 +    }

       557 +    generateImageIndexHtml(productData, images) {

⏺ Perfect! I've fixed the async message passing timeout issue. Here's what I've implemented to resolve the error:

  🔧 Fixed: Async Message Passing Timeout

  ✅ Root Cause Identified:

  The error "A listener indicated an asynchronous response by returning true, but the message channel closed before a 
  response was received" was caused by:
  1. Long-running operations without proper timeout handling
  2. Unhandled promise rejections in the background script
  3. Missing error boundaries for async operations

  🚀 Improvements Made:

  Background Script Enhancements:

  1. Better Message Handling:
  // Added proper timeout handling for long operations
  const timeoutPromise = new Promise((_, reject) => {
    setTimeout(() => reject(new Error('Operation timed out after 30 seconds')), 30000);
  });

  // Race condition with timeout for critical operations
  result = await Promise.race([
    this.downloadImage(message.url, message.filename, message.productId),
    timeoutPromise
  ]);

  2. Optimized Download Process:
  // Added delays between downloads to prevent overwhelming
  if (i > 0) {
    await new Promise(resolve => setTimeout(resolve, 200));
  }

  // Better error handling for each step
  try {
    console.log('📋 Creating product data manifest...');
    // ... manifest creation
    console.log('✅ Manifest created');
  } catch (error) {
    console.error('❌ Failed to create manifest:', error);
    // ... error handling
  }

  3. Comprehensive Error Boundaries:
  // Every operation now has proper try-catch
  try {
    const downloadId = await chrome.downloads.download({...});
    console.log(`✅ Downloaded ${i + 1}/${images.length}: ${indexedFilename}`);
  } catch (error) {
    console.error(`❌ Failed to download image ${i + 1}:`, error);
    // ... graceful error handling
  }

  Content Script Enhancements:

  1. Explicit Timeout Handling:
  // Added 60-second timeout with explicit error handling
  const result = await new Promise((resolve, reject) => {
    const timeout = setTimeout(() => {
      reject(new Error('Download request timed out after 60 seconds'));
    }, 60000);

    chrome.runtime.sendMessage({...}, (response) => {
      clearTimeout(timeout);

      if (chrome.runtime.lastError) {
        reject(new Error(chrome.runtime.lastError.message));
      } else if (response) {
        resolve(response);
      } else {
        reject(new Error('No response received from background script'));
      }
    });
  });

  2. Input Validation:
  if (!images || images.length === 0) {
    return {
      success: false,
      error: 'No images to download'
    };
  }

  🎯 Key Fixes:

  1. ⏱️ Timeout Management: 30-second timeout for background operations, 60-second for UI operations
  2. 🔄 Progressive Downloads: 200ms delay between image downloads to prevent rate limiting
  3. 🛡️ Error Boundaries: Every async operation wrapped in try-catch
  4. 📊 Better Logging: Step-by-step progress tracking with emojis for easy debugging
  5. ✅ Response Validation: Explicit checks for chrome.runtime.lastError and response validity

  🔍 What to Expect Now:

  - No more timeout errors - Operations will complete or fail gracefully
  - Better user feedback - Clear progress messages and specific error descriptions
  - Robust downloads - Images download with delays to prevent overwhelming the system
  - Graceful degradation - If some files fail, others will still download successfully

  The folder download should now work reliably, creating organized product folders with all images, data, and HTML gallery!

  class="__react_component_tooltip place-top type-dark tooltip" data-id="tooltip" style="left: 788px; top: 490px;">Number of 
  days for the product to be delivered after being shipped.</div></div><p class="sc-cmaqmh kOUXxd">We have a 30-day return 
  policy, which means you have&nbsp;30 days after receiving your item to request a return. 
  To be eligible for a return, your item must be in the same condition that you received it, unworn or unused, with tags, and
   in its original packaging. You’ll also need the receipt or proof of purchase.&nbsp;  To start a return or refund, you can 
  contact us directly at&nbsp;customercare@inspecialhome.com. We always prioritise return &amp; refund related inquiries, but
   as we are currently experiencing high volume of inquiries, it is advised to title your email in the format of&nbsp;Refund 
  / Return + Your Order Number. Please do not reply to any automated emails like order confirmation, shipping updates, news 
  letters and etc. for return &amp; refund as they might be filtered. Items sent back to us without first requesting a return
   will not be accepted.&nbsp;If your return is accepted, we’ll send you an instructions on how and where to send your 
  package.&nbsp;

  Damages &amp; Issues
  Please inspect your order upon reception and contact us immediately within&nbsp;3 days if the item is defective, damaged or
   if you receive the wrong item, so that we can evaluate the issue and make it right.

  Missing Parcels
  Once a parcel is delivered, it is under the customer's custody and it is the customer's responsibility to keep it safe. If 
  you received a parcel delivered message but cannot find it anyway, please contact us via email: 
  customercare@inspecialhome.com within 7 days from the first day you receive the&nbsp; parcel delivered message so we could 
  inspect or send you a replacement&nbsp;

  Exceptions / non-returnable items
  Please note that any cancellation, refund or exchange when the item is in transit will not be accepted.

  Given the nature of the products and the current covid condition, certain types of items cannot be returned or refunded, 
  include intimate goods like drinkware, customized or made on demand products and gift items.

  It is customers' responsibility to make sure the address is correct, complete, permanent and can be reasonably delivered. 
  Any items missing, damaged or failed to deliver due to incorrect, incomplete or unaccessible address and relocation of 
  customer are not refundable either.

  It is the customers' responsibility to track the parcel and coordinate their time for delivery, reschedule the delivery or 
  collect the parcels themselves timely. Missing parcels or parcels being disposed by the local courier due to customers' 
  absence, failure to reschedule or failure to collect the items timely is not eligible for refund. Parcels being returned by
   the couriers due to multiple failed delivery attempt caused by customers' absence or failure to collect the parcels timely
   is only eligible for partial refund ( order value - returning shipping fee ).

  It is customers' responsibility to inspect the items upon receiving. In the circumstance of defective / damaged items, 
  please notify us within 7 days from the first day you receive the parcel delivered message. However, defective or damaged 
  items failed to file a refund / replacement request within the 7-days time frame is not eligible for refund or replacement.

  Exchanges 
  The fastest way to ensure you get what you want is to return the item you have, and once the return is accepted, make a 
  separate purchase for the new item.

  Refunds
  We will notify you once we’ve received and inspected your return, and let you know if the refund was approved or not. If 
  approved, you’ll be automatically refunded on your original payment method within 7 business days. Please remember it can 
  take some time for your bank or credit card company to process and post the refund too. If more than 15 business days have 
  passed since we’ve approved your return, please contact us at customercare@inspecialhome.com.
